 Let us know the story behind this terrible form of the mother: Once an Asura named Daruk pleased Brahma
 unke dwaara die gaye vardaan se vah devon or brahmanon ko pralay kii agni ke samaan dukh dene laga
 He stopped all religious rituals and established his kingdom in heaven
 sabhi devtaa, brahma or vishnu ke dham pahunche
 Brahma ji told that this evil will be killed only by a woman
 tab brahma, vishnu sahit sabhi dev stri rup dhar dusht daruk se ladane gaye
 But that monster was very powerful, he defeated them and drove them away
 brahma, vishnu samet sabhi dev bhagwaan shiv ke dham kailash parvat pahunche tathaa unhen daitya daruk ke vishay main bataaya
 Lord Shiva, listening to her, looked at Mother Parvati and said, i pray you for the interest of Kalyani world and for the slaughter of the evil Daruk
 yah sun maa parvati muskaraai or apane ek ansh ko bhagwaan shiv main pravesh karaayaa

 and Brahma from mother Maya of Bhagwati, he saw the goddess sitting near Shiva

 maa kaali ke lalat main teesraa netra or chandra rekha thi

 maa ke krodh kii jwaala se sampoorn lok jalane laga
 Seeing the world burning with his anger, Lord Shiva took the form of a child
 shiv shmashaan main pahunche or vahaan let kar rone lage
 When Mama Kali saw that child in form, she became fascinated by his form

 Lord Shiva also drank his anger along with milk

kis prakaar prasad kaa vishesh prayog karen?- ishwar kii krupa ko apane andar laane ke liye prasad chadhaaya or grahan kiya jaataa he- prasad ke bina bhi puja ho sakati he , par prasad ho to zyada acha hoga- prasad main koi bhi satvik chiz , fal , mithai yahan tak jal bhi chadhaaya ja saktaa he- kuch na ho to shakkar chadhaanaa uttam hota he- safed prasad arpit karne se aarthik or maansik sthirataa aati he- bundi ke laddu arpit karne se samast grahon kii baadha shant hoti he- imarti kaa prasad durghatnaon or aakasmik ghatnaon se raksha karata he- panchamrita arpit karne aayu lambi hoti he , paapon kaa praayshchit hota he- keval jal arpit karne se shiksha , santan or ishwar kii krupa milti hapuja main phool arpit karnaa kitna aavashyak he? iskaa kya vishesh prayog he?- ishwar ko phool chadhaakar ham apni bhavanaayen vyakt karte hai

 Google Doodle par aaj childrence de (children's Day) manaaya ja rahaa he
 On this day the first and former Prime Minister Jawaharlal Nehru was born
 google ne ye doodle chachaa nehru (chacha Nehru) ko samarpit kiya he
 Let me tell you, this Google Doodle is made by Divyanshi Singhal, a seven year old girl studying in the second class of Gurugram
 divyanshi ne is tasviir main ped-paudhon ko chalate hue dikhaaya he or naam diya he 'walking tree' (walking Tree)
 Since 2009, every year on 14 November, Google holds a competition named 'doodle 4 Google'
 is saal is compitishan kii theme thi "when i grow up, i hope"
 Google 1 in this Children's Day competition
 1 lakh entries mili, ye sabhi chitra 1 se 5tak kii kaksha vaale bacchon ne banaae the, jisamen divyanshi singhl kii is painting ko chunaa gaya
